# 1024 Neurocontrol Lattice

## Purpose

This atlas materializes pass 5 as a full `1024`-fiber governance surface.

Address form:

`NeuroFiber(Microcell, Surface)`

Example:

`N11-C-R-Mf` = crystal-knot chamber repair manifest fiber

## Control Surfaces

- `Qn` = Queue
- `Lg` = Ledger
- `Pk` = Packet
- `Mf` = Manifest

## Lattice

## Zero Point

The `1024` lattice shows that every pass-4 microcell now carries four governance moods. The organism becomes deeper because no tissue can stay intelligent without also becoming accountable, transportable, and restart-safe.
